July 24, 2012**</u></strong></h2>\n<h3><strong><u><a href="http://pressbox.mlssoccer.com/content/new-playground-and-soccer-field-built-chester-part-att-mls-all-star-week-festivities">New playground and soccer field built in Chester as part of AT&amp;T MLS All-Star Week Festivities</a></u></strong></h3>\n<h2><strong><u>2012 AT&amp;T MLS All-Star Game Photos of The Day</u></strong></h2>\n<p><div class="field field-name-file field-type-file field-label-hidden"><div class="field-items"><div class="field-item even"><div class="styles file-styles large styles-field-file styles-style-large styles-container-image"><div class="media-thumbnail-frame"><img alt="" class="media-image" height="336" src="http://pressbox.mlssoccer.com/sites/g/files/g211536/f/styles/large/public/Kyle%20Beckerman%2C%20Graham%20Zusi%2C%20Carlos%20Valdes%20lend%20a%20hand.JPG?itok=VmfbrRJE" typeof="foaf:Image" width="480"/></div></div></div></div></div></p>\n<p>Photo Credit: Tony Quinn, MLSsoccer.com</p>\n<p><strong>Kyle Beckerman (Real Salt Lake), Graham Zusi (Sporting Kansas City) and Carlos Valdes (Philadelphia Union) lend a hand at today\xe2\x80\x99s MLS W.O.R.K.S. Playground Build at Science and Discovery High School in Chester, Pa. MLS All-Star players took part in youth activities and the construction of a playground and small-sided field. Major League Soccer joined the Philadelphia Union, AT&amp;T, Chester Upland School District and organizers from KABOOM! to construct this new playground and field for the Chester April 3, 2012**</u></h2>\n<pre>\n<strong><u>Sporting Kansas City goes 4-for-4; Next up \xe2\x80\x93 the defending champs, LA Galaxy, on ESPN (Sat., 4 p.m. ET)</u></strong>\n\nSporting Kansas City has won all four games to start their season, becoming just the sixth team in league history to do so. The LA Galaxy (1996, 1998, 2010), D.C. United (1997) and Real Salt Lake (2011) are the others to start 4-0. The Galaxy\xe2\x80\x99s 2010 win streak ended in Kansas City with a 0-0 tie.\n\nLos Angeles can return the favor on Saturday at LIVESTRONG Sporting Park (ESPN/Deportes, 4 p.m. ET).\n\nIf Kansas City produces another W in front of their boisterous home crowd, it will be the first time since 1998 (Los Angeles Galaxy started 9-0, first win came by shootout) that a club has earned five wins to start their season.  In 1996, the Galaxy earned eight straight wins in regulation to start the season before earning a shootout win over New England and extending that streak to 12-0 to start the season.</pre>\n<h2><u><u><u>**MLS News - March 27, 2012**</u></u></u></h2>\n<ul><li><h3><a href="http://pressbox.mlssoccer.com/content/week-mls-%E2%80%93-march-27-2012"><u>This Week in MLS - East makes a Comeback</u></a></h3></li></ul>\n<h2><u>**MLS News - March 20, 2012**</u></h2>\n<ul><li><h3><a href="http://pressbox.mlssoccer.com/content/week-mls-%E2%80%93-march-20-2012">This Week in MLS - Five hit Home this Week</a></h3></li></ul>\n<h2><u>**MLS News - March 15, 2012**</u></h2>\n<ul><li><h3>Game Guides now available for Week 2.
